if (is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird') && (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird') != '5a046d20ff561742a6145f73581bd04492a23e5b')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird');
	$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_3();
if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird');
} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird') != '5a046d20ff561742a6145f73581bd04492a23e5b') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird');
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'cac0cf1ecce1ce2c46f7c3a97de43a9e195e6992') {

		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}

	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'cac0cf1ecce1ce2c46f7c3a97de43a9e195e6992') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'cac0cf1ecce1ce2c46f7c3a97de43a9e195e6992') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/example_firebird.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/example_firebird.sql');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/example_firebird.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/example_firebird.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/example_firebird.sql') != '28f5a2937f80a261c1049f46b8f50c5a39e5c57f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/example_firebird.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/example_firebird.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/example_firebird.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_firebird.sql') !== '28f5a2937f80a261c1049f46b8f50c5a39e5c57f') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_firebird.sql') !== '1d64e0bd2dd9d4d3f501ed6a5543686d102e4dfb') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/example_firebird.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/example_firebird.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/example_firebird.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/example_firebird.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_firebird.sql') !== '28f5a2937f80a261c1049f46b8f50c5a39e5c57f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/example_firebird.sql');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct_firebird.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/struct_firebird.sql');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct_firebird.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/struct_firebird.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_firebird.sql') != '41cd823735f165b503b5b59533ae1195b8791c44') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_firebird.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/struct_firebird.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/struct_firebird.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_firebird.sql') !== '41cd823735f165b503b5b59533ae1195b8791c44') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_firebird.sql') !== 'b08548d95b4a3cf19be254cab7f96a92a44ac3f4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/struct_firebird.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/struct_firebird.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/struct_firebird.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/struct_firebird.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_firebird.sql') !== '41cd823735f165b503b5b59533ae1195b8791c44') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_firebird.sql');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_firebird.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/wellknown_country_firebird.sql');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_firebird.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/wellknown_country_firebird.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_firebird.sql') != '220d6fe4b66609f0aefb6e43ae0d6877c9aee991') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country_firebird.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/wellknown_country_firebird.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/wellknown_country_firebird.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_firebird.sql') !== '220d6fe4b66609f0aefb6e43ae0d6877c9aee991') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_firebird.sql') !== '1d64e0bd2dd9d4d3f501ed6a5543686d102e4dfb') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/wellknown_country_firebird.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/wellknown_country_firebird.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/wellknown_country_firebird.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/wellknown_country_firebird.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_firebird.sql') !== '220d6fe4b66609f0aefb6e43ae0d6877c9aee991') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country_firebird.sql');
		}
	}
}
